HUN_economic_crisis = {


	HUN_ask_for_help_from_britain = {

		icon = hol_attract_foreign_investors 

		allowed = { 
			original_tag = HUN
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_budget_management
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
					days < 365
				}
				has_country_flag = HUN_broke_trade_agreement_flag
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = HUN_available_trade_route_tt
				HUN_has_available_trade_route_eng = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_good_flag }
		}

		days_remove = 20

		cost = HUN_trade_deal_cost

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				tag = ENG
			}
		}

		visible = {
			HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_continue_bethlens_consolidation
				has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_council_of_commisars
				}
				has_completed_focus = HUN_trade_with_the_west
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_good_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_budget_management
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_need_to_stick_to_this_path_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_might_higher_agitation_tt
		}

		remove_effect = {
			#hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					country_event = { id = LH.33 days = 2 }
				}
			#}
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_receive_ressources_eng_tt
		}
	}

	HUN_cancel_trade_reliance = {	
		icon = generic_break_treaty
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_economic_crisis_good }
			}
			has_country_flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
		}
		
		available = {
			OR = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = { 
					tooltip = HUN_trade_1_5_years_tt
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
							days > 547
						}
					}
				}
				has_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_good_flag
			}
		}
		
		cost = 150
		
		days_remove = 30
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_cancel_trade_flag
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_economic_crisis_good_flag }
				HUN_reset_trade_deal_modifier = yes
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = HUN_cancel_trade_flag 
				clr_country_flag = HUN_already_trade_flag 
				clr_country_flag = HUN_trade_upgrade_flag 
				clr_country_flag = HUN_titan_trade_flag
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_remove_trade_tt
				custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_no_trade_5_years_tt
				set_country_flag = {
					flag = HUN_broke_trade_agreement_flag
					days = 1460
					value = 1
				}
				
				### REMOVE TRADE DEAL AND RESET ITS VALUES ###
				
				HUN_reset_trade_deal_modifier = yes 
				
				### REMOVE ANY BONUSES GAINED FROM TRADE DEAL ###
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = {
							flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
							days < 1270
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_loose_bonuses_tt
					HUN_remove_trade_deal_bonuses = yes
				}
				clr_country_flag = HUN_trade_deal_accepted_flag
				if = {
					limit = { 
						HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
							has_country_flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
						}
					}
					HUN_add_20_agitation = yes
					HUN_substract_15_influence_points = yes
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
						}
						every_country = {
							limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
							add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
						}
						GER = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
						}
						every_country = {
							limit = { is_in_faction_with = ITA }
							add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
						}
						ITA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					}
					clr_country_flag = HUN_ger_trade_partner_flag
					clr_country_flag = HUN_ita_trade_partner_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes 
						has_country_flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
						add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
					}
					SOV = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					clr_country_flag = HUN_sov_trade_partner_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = { 
						HUN_has_economic_crisis = yes 
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
							has_country_flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
							has_country_flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
						}
						every_country = {
							limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
							add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
						}
						ENG = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
						}
						every_country = {
							limit = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
							add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
						}
						FRA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
						}
						every_country = {
							limit = { is_in_faction_with = USA }
							add_opinion_modifier = { target = HUN modifier = HUN_GER_broke_trade_agreement }
						}
						USA = { remove_ideas = HUN_giving_economic_help }
					}
					clr_country_flag = HUN_eng_trade_partner_flag
					clr_country_flag = HUN_fra_trade_partner_flag
					clr_country_flag = HUN_usa_trade_partner_flag
				}
				add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 }
				set_country_flag = HUN_no_trade_partner_flag
			}
		}
	}
}

HUN_habsburg_empire_absolutism= {

	HUN_reinstate_absolutism = {
		icon = eng_abdication_crisis
		
		allowed = { 
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
		
		}
		
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_end_prime_ministry
			has_full_control_of_state = 70
			has_full_control_of_state = 973
			has_full_control_of_state = 4
			has_full_control_of_state = 9
		}
		
		days_remove = 70

		cost = 150

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		remove_effect = {
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_stability = 0.1
			set_country_flag = HUN_absolutism_established_flag
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = divisive_absolute_monarch
			add_country_leader_trait = autocratic_imperialist
		}
	}
	
	HUN_move_capital_to_vienna = {
		icon = eng_trade_unions_support
		
		allowed = { 
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			
		}
		
		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 4
		}
		
		days_remove = 70

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		remove_effect = {
			set_capital = { state = 4 }
			set_country_flag = HUN_moved_capital_flag
		}
	}
	
	HUN_take_control_over_military = {
		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans
		
		allowed = { 
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			
		}
		
		
		available = {
			has_army_experience > 70
		}
		
		days_remove = 20


		fire_only_once = yes
		
		remove_effect = {
			army_experience = -70
			set_country_flag = HUN_took_control_of_military_flag
			create_field_marshal = {
				name = "Albrecht Franz von Habsburg-Teschen"
				portrait_path = "gfx/leaders/HUN/Portrait_Hungary_Albrecht_von_Habsburg_Teschen.dds"
				traits = { german_sympathies harsh_leader }
				skill = 2
				attack_skill = 4
				defense_skill = 2
				planning_skill = 2
				logistics_skill = 2
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_riots_less_dangerous_tt
		}
	}
	
	HUN_solidify_control = {
		icon = generic_civil_support
		
		allowed = { 
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			#has_completed_focus = HUN_restore_first_empire
		}
		
		available = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_moved_capital_flag
			has_country_flag = HUN_absolutism_established_flag
		}
		
		days_remove = 50

		cost = 100

		fire_only_once = yes
		
		remove_effect = {
			unlock_national_focus = HUN_renounce_trianon_monarch
			set_country_flag = HUN_solidify_control_flag
		}
	}
	
	HUN_empire_riots = {

		icon = generic_political_rally

		available = {
			 has_country_flag = HUN_solidify_control_flag 
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 70

		activation = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_restoration_aus_hun
			has_completed_focus = HUN_populist_habsburg 
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_restoration_aus_hun
		}		

		fixed_random_seed = no

		fire_only_once = no

		is_good = no

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_took_control_of_military_flag } }
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.21
					}
					40 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.22
					}
					20 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.23
					}
				}
			}
			
			else = {
				random_list = {
					25 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.21
					}
					25 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.22
					}
					25 = {
						country_event = wtt_manchukou_bandit_sabotage.23
					}
					25 = {
					
					}
				}
			
			}
			hidden_effect = {

HUN_red_terror = {

	
	
	HUN_root_out_communists_stability = {
		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_red_terror_state }
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		
		targets = { 155 972 }
		
		target_root_trigger = { tag = HUN }
		
		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view
		
		cost = 100
		
		fire_only_once = no
		days_remove = 6
		
		days_re_enable = 14
		
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_red_terror_management
			}
			
		}
		
		allowed = {
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = communism
			}
			FROM = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = HUN_red_terror_state
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_stability value = 0 compare = equals }
					}
				}	
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_red_terror_management
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_stability value = 0.1 }
			}
			
			### REMOVE MODIFIER ###
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_recruitable value = 0 compare = equals }
							check_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_build_speed value = 0 compare = equals }
							check_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_stability value = 0 compare = equals }
						}
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_red_terror_state }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = HUN_red_terror_management
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_red_terror_stability_tt
			
			hidden_effect = {
				add_stability = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
	
	
	HUN_root_out_communists_war_sup = {
		icon = generic_arrest
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_red_terror_state }
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}

			}

							check_variable = { var = hun_red_terror_build_speed value = 0 compare = equals }

					}
				}
				FROM = {

				}
			}
			
			clr_country_flag = HUN_red_terror_management
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_red_terror_war_sup_tt
		}

	HUN_nagyvarad_artillery_cadet_school = {

		icon = ger_military_buildup

		available = {
			
			has_completed_focus = HUN_ludovica_academy
			
			has_full_control_of_state = 76
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = HUN_small_arms
				has_completed_focus = HUN_mobile_foc
			}
			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_expanding_schools_flag
			}
		}
	
		allowed = {
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_ludovica_academy
			#OR = {
			#	has_completed_focus = HUN_small_arms
			#	has_completed_focus = HUN_mobile_foc
			#}
			
		}

		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 70
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_expanding_schools_flag
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea = HUN_ludovica_academy_expanded}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = HUN_ludovica_academy_expanded
					add_idea = HUN_artillery_school
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_idea = HUN_sopron_pecs_school}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = HUN_sopron_pecs_school
					add_idea = HUN_artillery_school_2
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = HUN_expanding_schools_flag
		}
	}

political_actions = {

	HUN_integrate_the_move_political = { 
	
		icon = eng_trade_unions_demand
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 49
			command_power > 49
		}

		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_50_pp_50
		
		days_remove = 21
		
		available = {
			
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
			NOT = {
				has_power_balance = {
					id = HUN_fascist_tree_bop
				}
			}
			has_completed_focus = HUN_strengthen_the_hungarist_movement
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_move_integrated_flag
			}
			has_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = HUN_move_dynamic_modifier
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -50
				add_political_power = -50
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_remove_move_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_move_dynamic_modifier }

HUN_change_side_decisions = {
	
	HUN_contact_the_allies = { 
		
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		fire_only_once = no
		
		cost = 70
		
		days_remove = 21
		
		days_re_enable = 365
		
		visible = {
			is_faction_leader = no # you shouldn't be able to betray your own faction
			original_tag = HUN
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_panzerfaust_succeeded_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hungary_has_flipped_sides_flag }
		}
		
		available = {
			has_idea = HUN_miklos_horthy_jr
			is_faction_leader = no
			has_capitulated = no
			any_country = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_war_with = HUN
				OR = {
					has_government = democratic
					original_tag = ENG
					original_tag = USA
				}
			}
			has_government = neutrality
			NOT = {
				FACTION_LEADER  = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = hungary_has_flipped_sides_flag } #Hungary shouldn't be able to keep switching sides all the time
			}
			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
		
			clr_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_germans_might_find_out_tt
			
			
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				save_global_event_target_as = hungary_former_ally
			}
			
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = HUN
						has_government = democratic
						OR = {
							original_tag = ENG
							is_in_faction_with = ENG
						}
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = HUN
						has_government = democratic
						OR = {
							original_tag = ENG
							is_in_faction_with = ENG
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = hungary_new_ally
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						has_country_flag = HUN_italy_capitulated_so_peace_flag 
						has_country_flag = HUN_peace_second_time_flag 
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					random_list = {
						30 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # England receives the offer
						70 = { 
							if = {
								limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
								country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
								country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
							}
							else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						}  #Germany finds out 
					}
				}
			}
			
			
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
				}
				random_list = {
					80 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # England receives the offer
					20 = { 
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					}  #Germany finds out 
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 70 compare = greater_than_or_equals } is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # England receives the offer
					80 = { 
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					} #Germany finds out 
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					50 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # England receives the offer
					50 = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					} #Germany finds out  
				}
			}
		}
			 
	}
	
	HUN_approach_soviets = {
		
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		cost = 70
		
		days_remove = 21
		
		days_re_enable = 365
		
		allowed = {
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		available = {
			
			is_faction_leader = no
			has_capitulated = no
			any_country = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				has_war_with = HUN
				OR = {
					has_government = communism
					original_tag = SOV
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				FACTION_LEADER  = {
					has_government = communism
				}
			}
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = hungary_has_flipped_sides_flag } #Hungary shouldn't be able to keep switching sides all the time
			}
			
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = HUN_panzerfaust_succeeded_flag }
			is_faction_leader = no # you shouldn't be able to betray your own faction
			original_tag = HUN
			NOT = { has_country_flag = hungary_has_flipped_sides_flag }
			#hidden_trigger = { has_country_flag = can_change_sides_com }
		}
		
		cost = 0
		
		fire_only_once = yes
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_germans_might_find_out_tt
			clr_country_flag = HUN_sent_delegation_flag
			#save current faction leader for use in the event
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
					save_global_event_target_as = hungary_former_ally
				}
			}
			#top priority is joining the Commintern if they still exist
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = HUN
						has_government = communism
						OR = {
							original_tag = SOV
							is_in_faction_with = SOV
						}
					}
				}
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = HUN
						has_government = communism
						OR = {
							original_tag = SOV
							is_in_faction_with = SOV
						}
					}
					save_event_target_as = hungary_new_ally
				}
			}
			#then attempts to join any communist faction
			else = {
				random_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						has_war_with = HUN
						has_government = communism
					}
					save_event_target_as = hungary_new_ally
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 30 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
				}
				random_list = {
					80 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # Soviet Union receives the offer
					20 = { 
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					}  #Germany finds out 
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER =  { check_variable = { var = ger_alignment_influence value = 70 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # Soviet Union receives the offer
					80 = { 
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					} #Germany finds out 
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					50 = { event_target:hungary_new_ally = { country_event = { id = LH.197 hours = 24 } } } # Soviet Union receives the offer
					50 = {
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_margarete_succeeded_flag }
							country_event = { id = LH.271 hours = 24 }
							country_event = { id = LH.272 days = 5 } 
						}
						else = { country_event = { id = LH.196 hours = 24 } }
						#set_country_flag = HUN_germany_found_out_flag 
					} #Germany finds out  
				}
			}
			
			
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

	}

HUN_fascist_insurgency = {

	HUN_fascist_gaining_momentum = {
	
		icon = revolt
	
		selectable_mission = no
		
		is_good = no
		
		days_mission_timeout = 180
	
		allowed = {
			tag = HUN
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = HUN
		}
		
		available = {
			OR = {
				fascism < 0.20
				has_government = fascism
				has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
				has_completed_focus = HUN_reinstate_osiseg
				has_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_imprisoned_flag
			}
			
		}
		
		activation = {
			fascism > 0.20
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = HUN_boszormeny_coup_flag
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = HUN_populist_habsburg
					has_completed_focus = HUN_social_reforms
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_imprisoned_flag
			}
		}
		
		timeout_effect = {
		
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						fascism > 0.20
						fascism < 0.25
					}
				}
				add_popularity =  { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.08}
				activate_mission = HUN_fascist_gaining_momentum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						fascism > 0.25
						fascism < 0.30
					}
				}
				add_popularity =  { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05}
				activate_mission = HUN_fascist_gaining_momentum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						fascism > 0.30
						fascism < 0.35
					}
				}
				add_popularity =  { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.04}
				activate_mission = HUN_fascist_gaining_momentum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						fascism > 0.35
						fascism < 0.50
					}
				}
				add_popularity =  { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.03}
				activate_mission = HUN_fascist_gaining_momentum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					fascism > 0.5
				}
				set_temp_variable = { civil_war_strength = party_popularity@fascism }
				
				start_civil_war = {
					#ruling_party = ROOT
					ideology = fascism
					size = var:civil_war_strength
					capital = 154
					states = { 
						
					}
					#keep_political_leader = yes
				}
				
				every_enemy_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = HUN
						original_tag = HUN
					}
					load_focus_tree = LH_fascist
					complete_national_focus = HUN_empower_the_far_right
					complete_national_focus = HUN_fuse_the_right_wing_parties_under_szlasi
					complete_national_focus = HUN_plan_for_the_building_of_the_hungarian_state
					complete_national_focus = HUN_proclaim_szlasi_the_leader_of_the_nation_fascism
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			
		}
		
	
	}

}

							value = -0.15
						}

					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					power_balance_value = {
						id = HUN_fascist_tree_bop
						value > 0
					}
				}
				random_list = {

							value = 0.15
						}

	HUN_elni_es_nem_pusztulni = { 
	
		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		cost = 20
		
		days_remove = 14
		
		days_re_enable = 50
		
		available = {
			power_balance_value = {
				id = HUN_fascist_tree_bop
				value < -0.1
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_szalasi_decisions_flag
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = HUN_fascist_tree_bop
				value = 0.05
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = HUN_boszormeny_secures_local_farmers }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = HUN_boszormeny_secures_local_farmers
					days = -21
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = HUN_boszormeny_kills_hungarist_member }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = HUN_boszormeny_kills_hungarist_member
					days = -21
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = HUN_boszormeny_sways_hungarist_member }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = HUN_boszormeny_sways_hungarist_member
					days = -21
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_active_mission = HUN_boszormeny_attacks_factory }
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = HUN_boszormeny_attacks_factory
					days = -21
				}
			}
		}
	}

	HUN_construct_work_camps = {
		icon = generic_factory
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		cost = 0
		
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = HUN_forced_labor_flag
		}
		
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 8
		}
		
		days_remove = 30
		
	}
	
	HUN_construct_sorg_factory = { 
	
		icon = generic_factory
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		cost = 0
		
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 4
		}
		
		visible = {
			always = no
		}
		
		days_remove = 123
		
		remove_effect = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = HUN_sorg_bonus
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = construction_tech
			}
			clr_country_flag = HUN_special_factory_construction_flag
			set_country_flag = HUN_sorg_completed_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = HUN_economic_crisis_good_intro_tt
			set_variable = { var = HUN_crisis_global_building_slots_factor value = 0.1 tooltip = global_building_slots_factor_tt }
		}
	}

				has_country_flag = HUN_investing_in_army_flag
			}
		}

		}

			}
			set_country_flag = HUN_investing_in_army_flag
		}

				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = HUN_investing_in_army_flag

HUN_foreign_industrial_aid_category = {

	HUN_building_factory = {

		icon = generic_construction 

		fire_only_once = no
		
		allowed = { tag = HUN always = no }
		
		available = {
			always = no
		}

		is_good = yes
		
		selectable_mission = no

		days_mission_timeout = 40

		
		timeout_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = HUN_asking_titan_flag
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_investment_buda_can_start_flag }
				973 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 2
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = HUN_investment_buda_can_start_flag
				clr_country_flag = HUN_budapest_factory_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_investment_gyor_succeeded_flag }
				155 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = HUN_investment_gyor_can_start_flag
				clr_country_flag = HUN_gyor_factory_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = HUN_investment_szeged_succeeded_flag }
				972 = {
					add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes

	HUN_nationalise_the_industry = {
	
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 49
			has_political_power > 149
		}

		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_CP_50_PP_150
		
		icon = generic_civil_support
		
		fire_only_once = yes 
		
		days_remove = 70
		
		available = {
			has_government = fascism
			972 = {
				NOT = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = HUN_red_terror_state }
				}
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
		
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -50
				add_political_power = -150
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			set_country_flag = HUN_industry_nationalised_flag
			
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 972
						state = 973
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			
			custom_effect_tooltip = remove_industrial_concern 
			show_ideas_tooltip = HUN_maort
		}
		
	}

HUN_organize_the_blackshirts = {

	HUN_urge_restraint = {

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

		available = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_march_timer_flag }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_restrained_march_flag }
		}

		cost = 25

		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			ENG = {
				add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = -0.01 }
			}
			119 = { set_state_flag = ENG_has_blackshirt_support }
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_urge_restraint_tt
			set_country_flag = ENG_restrained_march_flag
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_speech_against_germany_tt
			
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

	HUN_blackshirt_march_in_northern_ireland = {

		icon = eng_blackshirt_march

		available = {
			ENG = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_march_timer_flag } has_full_control_of_state = 119 }
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = { state = 119 } 
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 26

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			ENG = {
				NOT = { has_government = fascism }
			}
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			119 = { save_event_target_as = ENG_blackshirt_march_state }
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					ENG = { country_event = { id = mtg_britain.57 days = 1 } }
					effect_tooltip = {
						add_stability = -0.041
						add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.027 }
					}
				}
				50 = {
					ENG = { country_event = { id = mtg_britain.58 days = 1 } }
					effect_tooltip = {
						add_stability = -0.054
						add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.027 }
					}
				}
				25 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.2
						has_country_flag = ENG_restrained_march_flag
					}
					ENG = { country_event = { id = mtg_britain.59 days = 1 } }
					effect_tooltip = {
						add_stability = -0.081
						add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.027 }
					}
				}
			}
